Here is the situation:\\ \tt \\ \tt WHAT: Things at places\\ \tt LEFT: shorts\\ \tt RIGHT: violin\\ \tt TOP: suit\\ \tt BOTTOM: flute\\ \tt CENTER: orchid\\ \tt NORTHWEST: dress\\ \tt NORTHEAST: helium\\ \tt SOUTHWEST: marimba\\ \tt SOUTHEAST: glue\\ \tt HERE: crayons\\ \tt THERE: spider\\ \tt NOWHERE: clips\\ \tt EVERYWHERE: flip-flops\\ \tt INSIDE: trivet\\ \tt OUTSIDE: tennis shoes\\ \tt \\ \tt Questions from the questioner will start with QUESTIONER. Please reply in the form: ANSWER: <some text>\\ \tt \\ \tt I will also ask you questions. These questions will start with ME: . Please answer these questions with: ASIDE: <some text>\\ \tt \\ \tt Important: Give short, direct answers!\\ \tt \\ \tt Let us start.

	   } 
	 & & \\ 
 

    \theutterance \stepcounter{utterance}  

    & & & \multicolumn{2}{p{0.3\linewidth}}{\cellcolor[rgb]{0.95,0.95,0.95}{%
	\makecell[{{p{\linewidth}}}]{% 
	  \tt {\tiny [GM$|$GM]}  
	 End probing 
	  } 
	   } 
	   } 
	 & & \\ 
 

    \theutterance \stepcounter{utterance}  

    & & & \multicolumn{2}{p{0.3\linewidth}}{\cellcolor[rgb]{0.95,0.95,0.95}{%
	\makecell[{{p{\linewidth}}}]{% 
	  \tt {\tiny [GM$|$GM]}  
	 Game finished. 
	  } 
	   } 
	   } 
	 & & \\ 
 

\end{supertabular}
}
